| You can follow later                                                                    | 您可以稍后关注                                 |
| You cannot come                                                                         | 你不能来                                       |
| You cannot come now                                                                     | 你现在不能来                                   |
| You cannot go with me                                                                   | 你不能跟我一起去                               |
| You clean outside but inside is dirty                                                   | 你清洁外面但里面很脏                           |
| You have heard “Thou shalt not kill”                                                    | 你听说过“不可杀人”                             |
| You know better                                                                         | 你更清楚                                       |
| You must be born again                                                                  | 你必须重生                                     |
| You saw no similitude the day                                                           | 你那天没有看到相似之处                         |
| You send forth your spirit                                                              | 你发出你的灵                                   |
| You shall know the truth, and the truth shall set you free                              | 你们必晓得真理，真理必叫你们自由               |
| You shall not kill                                                                      | 不可杀人                                       |
| You shall not sacrifice with leavened bread                                             | 不可与有酵的饼一同献祭                         |
| You shall not seethe a kid in mother's milk                                             | 不可用山羊羔母的奶煮山羊羔                     |
| You shall seek me but not find me                                                       | 你们要寻找我，却找不到我                       |
| You were perfect until                                                                  | 你曾经很完美，直到                             |
| You who follow must pay price                                                           | 跟随者必将付出代价                             |
| You will be with me                                                                     | 你会和我在一起                                 |
| You will bring the first fruits of the fruits                                           | 你将带来第一批果实                             |
| You will look for me and you cannot find me                                             | 你会寻找我，却找不到我                         |
| You will not leave Easter food until morning                                            | 你不会把复活节食物留到早上                     |
| You will reap what you sow                                                              | 种瓜得瓜，种豆得豆                             |
| You will seek me and you will find me, if you search                                    | 你们会寻找我，并且会找到我，只要你们寻找       |
| You will water them in the river of your pleasures...                                   | 你将在你的快乐之河中浇灌他们……                 |
| You'll be beaten in synagogues                                                          | 你会在犹太教堂里被殴打                         |
| You'll be brought before councils                                                       | 你将被带到议会                                |
| Your ears hear: ‘this is way’                                                           | 你的耳朵听到：“这就是方法”                     |
| Your hand to find out enemies                                                           | 用你的手找出敌人                               |
| Your kingdom come, will be done                                                         | 愿祢的国降临，愿祢的国成就                     |
| Your sons and daughters will be held captive                                            | 你的儿子和女儿将被俘虏                         |
| Yours is greatness                                                                      | 你是伟大的                                     |
| Yours is the kingdom, Lord                                                              | 主啊，国度是你的                               |
| Zaccheus up a tree                                                                      | 撒该爬上树                                     |
| Zaccheus' conversion                                                                    | 撒该的转变                                     |
| Zacharias' doubt                                                                        | 撒迦利亚的怀疑                                 |
| Zacharias' dream                                                                        | 撒迦利亚的梦                                   |
| Zacharias' ministry                                                                     | 撒迦利亚的事工                                 |
| Zechariah's prophecy                                                                    | 撒迦利亚的预言                                 |
| Zechariah's prophecy fulfilled                                                          | 撒迦利亚的预言应验了                           |
| Zophar repeats advice                                                                   | 琐法重复劝告                                   |
| Zophar, the third friend                                                                | 琐法，第三个朋友                               |
